	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql') != 'c37404ef48d85c0ddfef211c3fd11bd626478a17') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql') !== 'c37404ef48d85c0ddfef211c3fd11bd626478a17') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql') !== '50d1056b5b650235463be6acf9569b23735dcf51') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql') !== 'c37404ef48d85c0ddfef211c3fd11bd626478a17') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/access/sql/example.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql') != '532f5fe81b2b0841f00b9191566f5ea3d626c923') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql') !== '532f5fe81b2b0841f00b9191566f5ea3d626c923') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql') !== '1fec68d72376732d0619447cdaac3115a631e954') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql') !== '532f5fe81b2b0841f00b9191566f5ea3d626c923') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mssql/sql/struct.sql');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql') != '6167697b8d84e032fe76dfd6f854cf775ccb3de2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql') !== '6167697b8d84e032fe76dfd6f854cf775ccb3de2') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql') !== '8ae1fb7c0879ff288771e213b2c87739d04062f2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql') !== '6167697b8d84e032fe76dfd6f854cf775ccb3de2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/example.sql');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql') != '40383a0919f435b286d311c67c2754c03c675d8e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql') !== '40383a0919f435b286d311c67c2754c03c675d8e') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql') !== 'dfd0bbe51490a0cab16319a5e596a8833b5d9293') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql') !== '40383a0919f435b286d311c67c2754c03c675d8e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/mysql/sql/struct.sql');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql') != '145f80ae7b22c5086190fdb04ab7a874f19ef195') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql') !== '145f80ae7b22c5086190fdb04ab7a874f19ef195') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql') !== '08924543352136fb7a3881e85b8ac834286035c7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql') !== '145f80ae7b22c5086190fdb04ab7a874f19ef195') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/oracle/sql/example.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql') != '551f5aa84b7b3e85f971095cffc7b0b7ba2010ce') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql') !== '551f5aa84b7b3e85f971095cffc7b0b7ba2010ce') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql') !== 'edf3443e1f747a139d731eae0e020de644d45a18') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql') !== '551f5aa84b7b3e85f971095cffc7b0b7ba2010ce') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/sql/example.sql');
